<span id="freeTextContainer2505545356714051857">2.5<br/>This is a tale of beauty and the beast, the horny, foul mouthed, crude, triple wiener pierced womanizing beast. <br/>Cage is a jerk, but he's an honest jerk. He tells his bed mate that he only wants to wet his wick and nothing more. It's too bad for him he tries to snuff the wick with his unstable girl of the moment. She is off the charts wacko and will do what ever it takes to get her man back.<br/>Melissa, is a strong independent woman with too much responsibly on her shoulders. She is raising her de</span>
  <span id="freeText2505545356714051857" style="display:none">2.5<br />This is a tale of beauty and the beast, the horny, foul mouthed, crude, triple wiener pierced womanizing beast. <br />Cage is a jerk, but he's an honest jerk. He tells his bed mate that he only wants to wet his wick and nothing more. It's too bad for him he tries to snuff the wick with his unstable girl of the moment. She is off the charts wacko and will do what ever it takes to get her man back.<br />Melissa, is a strong independent woman with too much responsibly on her shoulders. She is raising her dead sisters son, supporting herself her nephew and her mother on little pay and long hours. She only wants pleasures from a man, not more. <br />When "it" hits the fan, Cage is the one anyone would want on their side. he take serious measures to fix the problem without mercy. His ties to his past are there to help him when he calls, and boy do they come though.<br />I had a hard time with the first 50% of the story. Cage was so crude, cold and cutthroat to his bed mate. I own my own little trucker mouth but dang it if he didn't even make my eyes want to turn away and cringe. Cage was just nasty. He wasn't the Greg Cage I met in book one, he was amped up big time, and I didn't like him again till the end of the story. The sex was cold and ugly with girl #1 and hot and steamy with beauty. I liked book #1 much more than this one it just went too far for my taste. I'm giving the next book, Beck a try.</span>

  <blockquote> 6 "smoking hot, decorated down under, panty melting" stars </blockquote>
</b><br><br>So you all know how I feel about Axel. I love him. I was his #1 princess. We had it all, right? Well you see I secretly had a thing for Greg, but I knew it wasn't going any where. I had Axel, he made me happy, we had a future. I loved him. <br><br>Sometimes love isn't enough. From the very beginning, Greg Cage owned me. I couldn't resist his charm, his muscles, his sex appeal and lets be honest, him being decorated 3 times, doesn't make me want to run away. It makes me want to run right up to him and beg for him to make me his beauty. <br><br><a href="http://s1331.photobucket.com/user/bookobsessedmomof3/media/photo22_zpsb4a288ac.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>So, I started a thing with him. I couldn't just walk away, he owned me. Have you ever had a person see inside your soul, make you feel things you never thought you could feel? well that's what Cage did to me. I'm not a good person, but damn does Cage make me feel GOOOODDDD<br><br>Now, I share, I was taught to share, unlike Melissa. We had words and we have come to an agreement. I will not go into this agreement cause that bitch scares me. Did you see how she handled Mandy. FUCK. when I see her coming I run the other way. She is one badass chick. I love her. Its refreshing to meet someone who has her head on straight, can beat a bitch down, says what is exactly what is on her mind but then cuddle up next to her man and be sweet. <br><br><a href="http://s1331.photobucket.com/user/bookobsessedmomof3/media/photo_zps253a6efb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>While all the shit went down, you will know what shit i'm talking about when you read his damn book, which you should have done or are doing right now, I had sometime to reflect on my other relationship with Mr. Braxxon. Now see Cage and him have a past, and I was apart of that past. Braxx taught me a lot and seeing him again just brought back all my feelings and scared me, ALOT. thankfully he wasn't around for very long, just long enough to make me want him again. But then he vanished and I was left all hot and bothered, cause damn him and cage together was fucking hot. I'd like to lock them in a room together and go all 50 shades on their find ass, together, at the same time. wait I got side tracked. <br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/sons%20of%20anarchy" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

              <span id="reviewTextContainer710882258" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17436099711812120879"><b>I flipping love this book!!!</b><br/><br/>I connected with both Melissa and Cage from the very beginning. They met at sort of a love at first sight or in Cage's opinion:<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Hard on at first sight</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>Their connection was <b>hot</b>. As their story progressed, you can feel the relationship growing and how they are connected in more than just body parts.<br/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380435412ra/879631.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>There was too many things I loved about this book.   <b>
    <i>Never thought I would need a break, but my dick is tir</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText17436099711812120879" style="display:none"><b>I flipping love this book!!!</b><br><br>I connected with both Melissa and Cage from the very beginning. They met at sort of a love at first sight or in Cage's opinion:<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Hard on at first sight</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Their connection was <b>hot</b>. As their story progressed, you can feel the relationship growing and how they are connected in more than just body parts.<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380435412ra/879631.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>There was too many things I loved about this book. Loved how the guys talk among each other (ah Axel!)<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Never thought I would need a break, but my dick is tired man</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Loved how the story played out, LOVED Alpha, protective Cage. (The Perfect Book Boyfriend!) and Loved the kids (I know there will be more *winks*)<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>When I get big like you, will my wiener be big too?</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>When I read Axel, I couldn't help but compare it with a KA book, but with Cage, not once did I make the comparison. <br><br>Anyway this was an amazing sequel and it surpassed any high expectations I had. Harper Sloan is one mean author and this book gave us snippets of Beck and Maddox's book and I cannot wait!!!<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435412i/879632.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> I want Maddox!!!</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('MF3YrMXvcKCVXTGsoR4tWEs5wEch3tTCkOyOycCrLvb9gBKhAiRX9GfIEfKR1rAZHORmTImBGoUZXt2YFjLFEQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('MWnv/QAOo26IQoYuXDTMesh7TB6AzOoBQAUVYvwtJzT8tCXwx8WEOnrXpnBs/FE7n6bqFSiTJEbJt0YzKrTM0w==')})
  }
